<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:overeen.html>overeen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">equal, matching</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stemmen.html>stemmen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to tune, to adjust</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To be tuned (especially instruments), accorded</li></ol>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> switch, shift (from one thing or status to another)

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">overliden</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">overlīthan</i>. </p>

***overlord.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:overlord.html>overlord</a> (101623)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:over-.html>over-</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">lord</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:overlord.html>overlord</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">overlords</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A ruler of other rulers.
<dl><dd><i>The various tribal chieftains <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> each spring to elect an <b><a href = vnd.unilang:overlord.html>overlord</a></b> that would lead them in time of war.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> In the English feudal system, a lord of a manor who <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> subinfeudated a particular manor, estate or fee, to a tenant.
<dl><dd><i>The tenant thenceforth owed to the <a href = vnd.unilang:overlord.html>overlord</a> one of a variety of services, usually military service or serjeanty, depending on which form of tenure the estate <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:held.html>held</a> under.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li>Anyone with overarching power or authority in a given domain.
<dl><dd><i>The crusty old <a href = vnd.unilang:professor.html>professor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:overlord.html>overlord</a></b> of the history department, and few dared to cross his will.</i></dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2009</b>,  Charles Stross,  <cite>The Jennifer Morgue</cite>, page 239:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Fluffy <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> wearing a diamond collar that <a href = vnd.unilang:belongs.html>belongs</a> in the Tower of London with a platoon of Beefeaters standing guard <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> it. "I for one welcome our new feline <b><a href = vnd.unilang:overlord.html>overlord</a></b>s."</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">one with power or authority</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> This sense frequently <a href = vnd.unilang:carries.html>carries</a> negative connotations, and may imply tyranny or authoritarianism.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">overlady</span></li></ul>
